Every wall the multi-focal sprint set out to attack has either landed a closure (W1a first-pass production, W1b leading-order Layer-2, W1c at the screening mechanism, W2b-easy proof-sketched at the maturity Paper 38 had before L5 closed) or been cleanly named as frontier-of-field (W2a renormalization, W2b-medium/hard cross-manifold, W3 inner-factor calibration). The framework composes focal lengths via cross-register two-body coordinate operators built on the Roothaan 1951 closed form, anchored in a tensor-product propinquity-convergent NCG construction extending Paper 38. Open follow-ups: R1 + R2 keystone tightening; W1c-residual orthogonality wall; W1b magnetization-density operator-level construction; Pachucki higher-order match; MgH₂/HCl PES regression. Memos: `debug/multifocal_phase_a_synthesis_memo.md`, `debug/multifocal_b_{w1a,w1b,w1c,w2a,w2b,w3,position}_diag_memo.md` (seven Phase B diagnostics ~30,000 words), `debug/multifocal_phase_b_synthesis_memo.md`, `debug/multifocal_phase_c_positioning_memo.md`, `debug/multifocal_phase_c_w2b_easy_memo.md` (~600 lines), `debug/multifocal_phase_c_w1c_memo.md` (~3500 words), `debug/multifocal_phase_c_w1a_physics_memo.md`.

- **Precision catalogue extension — Muonium 1S-2S and Positronium 1S HFS (Track 1 of post-MH multi-track launch, 2026-05-08):** two-observable extension of the multi-focal precision arc to round out the e/μ/p mass-hierarchy matrix. **Muonium 1S-2S (e⁻ on μ⁺):** Mu-MASS Crivelli 2018 measurement $\nu = 2{,}455{,}529{,}002.5(9.9)$ MHz reproduced at **−0.11 ppm** by pure rest-mass rescaling from H experimental ($\nu_H \times m_\text{red}(e\mu)/m_\text{red}(ep) = 2{,}455{,}528{,}721$ MHz), and at **−0.25 ppm** by framework Bohr+SE plus cross-register $V_{eN}$ recoil ($2{,}455{,}528{,}394$ MHz). The −0.11 ppm number is the headline: rest-mass projection theorem (Paper 34 §III.14) verified at sub-ppm between H and Mu, with the residual cleanly attributable to NLO recoil scaling differential ($m_p/m_\mu = 8.88\times$ between systems). Mu has no QCD nuclear structure (point antimuon → no Zemach, no FNS, no polarizability), making it the cleanest possible test of the framework's QED machinery: only LS-8a-class multi-loop QED inputs are external. Sprint MH-A/B (μH) tested e→μ swap at unchanged nucleus; this sprint tests the inverse, μ→e swap at unchanged lepton with 8.88× lighter nucleus. Files: `debug/precision_catalogue_muonium.{py,_memo.md}`, `debug/data/precision_catalogue_muonium.json`. **Positronium 1S HFS (e⁻e⁺ equal-mass):** Ishida 2014 measurement $\nu_\text{HFS} = 203.389$ GHz tested in the equal-mass limit $\lambda_a = \lambda_b = m_\text{red}(ee) = 0.5$. Framework-native Bohr-Fermi (spinor + Fermi-contact + Fock + rest-mass projection) captures the magnetic dipole-dipole part exactly: $\nu_F = (1/3) m_e c^2 \alpha^4 / h = 116.79$ GHz (machine-precision match to canonical formula). **The annihilation channel $e^+e^- \to \gamma \to e^+e^-$ contributes the remaining 3/12 of LO ($87.59$ GHz) but is NOT framework-native** — virtual-loop second-quantized field-theory effect, not generated by the framework's bare action. Same wall as Källén-Sabry two-loop VP for muonic H. Framework + Layer-2 annihilation = LO total $204.39$ GHz vs experimental $203.389$ GHz at +0.49% — multi-loop QED (Czarnecki-Melnikov-Yelkhovsky 2000, $\alpha^5 m_e c^2/h$) closes the rest. **New finding for the multi-focal architecture:** Roothaan multipole termination at $L_\text{max} = 2 \ell_\text{max}$ is preserved at the equal-mass limit. The termination is a Gaunt selection rule (angular content), not a small-parameter expansion — holds independently of $\lambda_a/\lambda_b$ ratio. Multi-focal architecture now verified across the full hierarchy: $\lambda_l \ll \lambda_n$ (H, asymptotic acceleration), $\lambda_l \sim \lambda_n$ (μH, comparable scales), $\lambda_l = \lambda_n$ (Ps, symmetric — no acceleration but Gaunt termination preserved). Files: `debug/precision_catalogue_positronium.{py,_memo.md}`, `debug/data/precision_catalogue_positronium.json`. **Catalogue updates:** Paper 34 §V gained two Mu rows (machine-precision, Two-projection chain); §V.B gained two Ps rows (off-precision, error code A) + one Mu row (rest-mass projection verification at varied nucleus mass). The structural-skeleton scope is verified empirically on a fourth and fifth precision system; together with H 21cm, μH Lamb, μH HFS, the e/μ/p mass-hierarchy matrix is now spanned. Each residual cleanly attributable to LS-8a-class multi-loop QED.

- **Chemistry-solver re-test (Track 2 of post-MH multi-track launch, 2026-05-08):** tests whether the multi-focal Phase C closures (balanced coupled + cross-center V_ne via Shibuya–Wulfman + screened W1c via `cross_center_screened_vne`) close, persist, or change the v2.0.32 baseline R_eq drift. **Combined verdict: first-row drift PERSISTS at Track CD level (Phase C is no-op for LiH); second-row W1c-residual orthogonality wall EMPIRICALLY CONFIRMED by NaH binding determination.** Architectural finding: the v2.0.32 baseline drift was diagnosed in the level-4 PK-composed PES solver (`composed_diatomic.py`); the Phase C closures live in the qubit-encoded balanced coupled architecture (`balanced_coupled.py`), which is structurally a different solver with no separate `l_max` parameter (basis enumerates at `(n,l,m)` with `l<n`, so `n_max` couples radial + angular). **The chemistry-solver upgrade the framework HAS already received is the balanced-coupled construction itself (Track CD, v2.0.39, April 2026), which reduced the original PK-composed wall (+0.18 bohr/l_max) by 3× to +0.054 bohr/n_max via cross-block ERIs + cross-center V_ne via Shibuya-Wulfman.** That upgrade shipped before Phase C; Phase C did not move it further for first-row. **First-row LiH (n_max=2):** W1c bit-identical at 5×10⁻¹⁴ Ha across 5-point PES grid — confirms the Phase C-W1c diagnostic claim that `_detect_core_type` returns `None` for Z<11 and the screened path collapses to bare path bit-precisely. n_max=2 reproduces Track CD baseline: R_eq = 3.227 bohr (Track CD: 3.226), R_err = 7.03% (Track CD: 7.0%), E_err = 1.71% (Track CD: 1.8%). n_max=3 single point at R=3.015 stalled in 4-electron FCI eigsh on 740k-determinant sparse matrix beyond fork compute budget; Track CD result (R_eq=3.280, drift +0.054 bohr/n_max) accepted as baseline. **Second-row NaH (n_max=2, Q=20, 2e FCI):** the single highest-value follow-up — Phase C D-PES regression confirmed 5.4-6.0× cross-V_ne reduction at NaH equilibrium but reportedly could not determine binding because n_e-projected FCI driver was not yet wired in. `coupled_fci_energy` IS that driver. NaH balanced FCI 7-point R-grid (R ∈ {2.5, 3.0, 3.5, 4.0, 5.0, 7.0, 10.0}) at max_n=2 ran in 7 seconds total. **Result: PES monotonically descends in BOTH `screened=False` (Sprint 7 baseline) AND `screened=True` (W1c)** — no internal minimum at any tested R, R_min sits at the smallest R-grid point in both cases. **W1c reduces edge-to-dissociation gap by 17.5×** (bare: −6.24 Ha; screened: −0.36 Ha), three times more than the 5.4-6× single-R diagnostic, but binding is NOT recovered. **The W1c-residual orthogonality wall named in Phase C is now empirically confirmed at the FCI level**: the H valence orbital ↔ [Ne]-core orthogonality (Phillips-Kleinman-class) sits beyond the Hartree screening of Z_eff(ρ) that W1c implements. The architectural difference between first-row binding and second-row non-binding is that first-row uses an explicit core block in the FCI sector (electrons resolve their own orthogonality), while second-row uses a frozen-core potential (orthogonality must be enforced externally; W1c does not yet do so). **The W1c-residual orthogonality wall is the single remaining engineering closure for second-row chemistry.** A Phillips-Kleinman-class projection on the H valence orbital against the [Ne] core in cross-center geometry is the mechanical fix. Files: `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih.py`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih_quick_nmax2.py`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih_nmax3.py`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_nah.py`, `debug/data/chemistry_solver_retest_lih.json`, `debug/data/chemistry_solver_retest_nah.json`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih_memo.md`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_synthesis_memo.md`.

- **Phillips-Kleinman cross-center sprint (post-Track-2 chemistry-solver follow-up, 2026-05-08):** named engineering closure for the W1c-residual orthogonality wall. **Verdict: HONEST NEGATIVE — PK reduces NaH descent depth from 0.357 Ha (W1c only) to 0.305 Ha at standard absolute-PK parameters ($E_v = 0$), a 14.6% improvement, but does NOT close the wall.** PES still monotonically descending, $R_\text{min}$ still at the smallest tested R (2.5 bohr), no internal equilibrium minimum. The W1c-residual orthogonality wall is structurally deeper than W1b alone. New module `geovac/phillips_kleinman_cross_center.py` (~280 lines, 21 tests passing) implements the standard PK operator-form approximation $\Delta H_{pq}^\text{PK} = \sum_c (E_v - E_c) S_{pc} S_{cq}$ with cross-center overlaps $S_{pc}$ via 2D Gauss-Legendre × radial-grid quadrature, real-SH azimuthal selection ($m_p^\text{signed} = m_c^\text{signed}$) enforced exactly, Clementi-Roetti HF eigenvalues for [Ne]-core orbitals (Na: $E_{1s} = -40.479$ Ha, $E_{2s} = -2.797$ Ha, $E_{2p} = -1.518$ Ha), direction-based rotation reusing `shibuya_wulfman._build_block_rotation_matrix`. Wired into `geovac/balanced_coupled.py` via `pk_cross_center: bool = False` and `pk_E_valence_ref: float = 0.0` kwargs (bit-exact backward compat when off, verified). 4-config NaH PES at n_max=2: bare 6.244 Ha descent → screened (W1c) 0.357 Ha → screened+PK 0.305 Ha → still 4× deeper than experimental $D_e \approx 0.075$ Ha. Strong-PK probe ($E_v$ scan) shows minimum-depth signature near $E_v = 100$ Ha (descent reduced to 0.148 Ha with hint at internal min) but this is unphysical parameter tuning. **Diagnosis of remaining wall:** candidate sources beyond W1c+W1b PK: (i) inner-core penetration physics (real H 1s tail in unscreened nucleus region), (ii) hydrogenic $Z_\text{orb}=1$ basis on the Na valence side being qualitatively wrong (it is not the actual Na 3s orbital but a generic $Z_\text{eff}=1$ hydrogenic function), (iii) cross-block ERI treatment between Na valence and H valence at mismatched effective charges. Most likely next engineering target: replace the $Z_\text{orb}=1$ basis on the Na center with radial Schrödinger eigenstates of the FrozenCore $Z_\text{eff}(r)$ potential (infrastructure already exists in `neon_core._solve_screened_radial`). Strict Schmidt orthogonalization is the mathematically definitive but expensive alternative. Paper 17 §6.10 gained "two solvers, two drift signatures" subsection (architectural clarification: drift lives in `composed_diatomic.py`, balanced is `balanced_coupled.py`). Paper 19 gained `\subsection{sec:w1c_residual}` documenting the W1c-residual wall, the PK cross-center engineering closure, the negative result with 4-config descent table, and the next-target diagnosis. Files: `geovac/phillips_kleinman_cross_center.py`, `tests/test_phillips_kleinman_cross_center.py` (21/21 passing), `debug/pk_cross_center_nah.py`, `debug/data/pk_cross_center_nah.json`, `debug/pk_cross_center_synthesis_memo.md`.

- **Sprint Mu Lamb shift (precision catalogue extension, 2026-05-08):** muonium 2S₁/₂-2P₁/₂ Lamb shift completes the e/μ/p mass-hierarchy matrix at four operating points. **Framework-native: $1047.63$ MHz vs Karshenboim 2005 theoretical reference $1047.49(5)$ MHz, residual $+0.135$ MHz / $+0.013\%$ — the cleanest one-loop QED match in the catalogue at this mass-hierarchy operating point.** Architecture: Paper 36 LS-1..LS-7 transferred verbatim to Mu under rest-mass projection (Paper 34 §III.14); $\beta = 2/(m_\text{red}\alpha) = 275.40$ vs 274.22 for normal H — same contact regime, full Uehling kernel and contact form agree to 0.24 MHz. **Pure rest-mass rescaling cross-check:** Paper 36 H framework value $1052.19 \times m_\text{red}(e\mu)/m_\text{red}(ep) = 1047.696$ MHz vs native compute $1047.625$ MHz — agreement to 0.071 MHz / 7 ppm, sharpest verification yet of the rest-mass projection theorem at the Lamb-shift bracket level. **Recoil-absorption observation:** the framework's pure Eides §3.2 SE bracket gives $+1074.13$ MHz; Karshenboim's "SE one-loop" itemization is $+1085.84$ MHz, separately-itemizing "Recoil NLO $-11.30$ MHz". The two differ by $\sim 0.4$ MHz — the framework's $m_\text{red}$ rescaling absorbs Karshenboim's itemized recoil at the bracket level, so naively adding the recoil to the framework total double-counts. **Why Mu Lamb shift is the cleanest of the four mass-hierarchy points:** (i) no FNS ($\mu^+$ point lepton), (ii) no QCD polarizability, (iii) Uehling regime in contact-form sweet spot, (iv) $m_\text{red} \approx 1$ keeps Eides bracket at calibration point, (v) recoil mixing absorbed into rescaling. The single Layer-2 multi-loop input (Karshenboim $\alpha^2(Z\alpha)^4$ at $+0.20$ MHz) is within the $+0.13$ MHz native residual — **the framework's one-loop QED is sufficient to reproduce Mu Lamb shift theory at sub-$0.05\%$ in this regime**. Mass-hierarchy comparison: H Lamb $-0.534\%$ (m_red≈1, m_n≈1836); μH Lamb $-0.92\%$ native / $-0.10\%$ +lit (m_red≈186, m_n≈1836); Mu 1S-2S $-0.11$ ppm (rest-mass rescaling); Mu Lamb $+0.013\%$ native (m_red≈1, m_n≈207). Paper 34 §V gained one machine-precision row (Mu Lamb framework-native +0.013%); §V.B gained one off-precision row (vs Mariam 1982 $1054(22)$ MHz exp at $-0.6\%$, within experimental uncertainty). Paper 36 §VIII gained `\subsection{sec:sprint_mu_lamb}` (architecture transfer, component decomposition, recoil-absorption note, mass-hierarchy matrix completion). - **Sprint CP² packing scoping (Track 3 of post-MH multi-track launch, 2026-05-08):** scoping pass on whether the Paper 0 packing axiom admits a faithful analog on natural compact homogeneous spaces beyond S³ — primary focus CP² = SU(3)/U(2) and the SU(3) (p,q) irrep lattice; secondary 5%-passes on S⁶ = G₂/SU(3), HP¹ = S⁴, CP³ = SU(4)/U(3), full flag SU(3)/T, OP² = F₄/Spin(9), Grassmannians. **Verdict: PARTIAL CLOSURE — does NOT land in the strong sense.** (a) The SU(3) (p,q) irrep lattice closes mathematically as a hexagonal-connectivity graph: 15 lattice points through level k=4, dim(p,q) = (p+1)(q+1)(p+q+2)/2, Casimir C₂(p,q) = (p²+q²+pq)/3 + (p+q), 6-neighbor adjacency from (1,0) ⊗ (p,q) = (p+1,q) ⊕ (p−1,q+1) ⊕ (p,q−1) and (0,1)-tensor — the triangular lattice the PI's QCD intuition pointed at. Cumulative state count Σ_{p+q=K} dim(p,q) = (K+1)(K+2)²(K+3)/12 (closed form, verified through K=4 by direct sum: 1, 6, 20, 50, 105). (b) CP² hosts the (p,p)-symmetric sub-lattice with Laplace–Beltrami spectrum λ_p = p(p+2) and multiplicities (p+1)³ (vs S³'s (p+1)² at the same eigenvalue — extra (p+1) factor is the Hopf-fibration U(1) direction). (c) **Neither closes from a packing-axiom motivation with the same epistemic standing as Paper 0.** Paper 0's axioms ("binary distinguishability + 2D isotropy") are **rank-1 specific**; they do not lift to rank 2 without becoming representation-theoretic. The "minimum to define a metric" argument has no SU(3) analog; the "isotropy → uniform density" axiom has no rank-2 analog (only SU(3)-equivariance, which is rep-theoretic input not packing-axiom input). The scaling rule (irrep dim formula) comes from Weyl's character formula, not annular-area counting. (d) **Coulomb/HO category obstruction confirmed at every higher-rank candidate:** Paper 24 §V four-layer asymmetry (spectrum-computing L_0; calibration π; Wilson-with-matter; combinatorial vocabulary) — CP²/(p,q) lattice sit at "layer-iv only" (combinatorial vocabulary without dynamics structure), structurally distinct from S³ (layers i–iv) and S⁵ Hardy (layer iii partial). Calibration π (κ = −1/16, K = π(B+F−Δ)) is S³-specific by Paper 23 §IV Fock rigidity theorem; does not transfer. (e) Eightfold-way correspondence (octet at (1,1) dim 8, decuplet at (3,0) dim 10, 27 at (2,2) dim 27) is **tautological**, not predictive — the (p,q) lattice contains the eightfold way *because* it is SU(3) rep theory by construction. (f) **Recommendation: do not prioritize CP² as the next major track.** Continue with Tracks 1 (multi-focal precision catalogue) and 2 (chemistry solver re-test). The (p,q) lattice and CP² spherical-rep tower remain available as secondary catalogue-style tools for organizing SU(3)-related observations within the existing framework. (g) **One non-tautological open question flagged:** the extra (p+1) Hopf-direction multiplicity on CP² could in principle host U(1) hypercharge × SU(3) color structure at the kinematic level if the U(1) direction has dynamical content — opportunistic 1-2 week sub-sprint scoped in §5.1 of memo. **Honest synthesis:** the "second packing axiom" question (W3 in CLAUDE.md §1.7 multi-focal-wall taxonomy) is **structurally distinct** from "find a packing on a different geometry" — whatever generates inner-factor calibration data does NOT need to be a packing-axiom analog on a higher-rank geometry, and this scoping does not move the W3 question. Files: `debug/cp2_packing_scoping_memo.md` (~5000 words, 5 sections), `debug/data/cp2_packing_scoping_results.json` (lattice + CP² + S³ comparison + eightfold-way correspondence tables).

- **Precision catalogue extension — Muonium 1S HFS (post-Phillips-Kleinman, 2026-05-08):** closes the muonium catalogue triple (1S-2S, 2S-2P Lamb, 1S HFS) by extending the framework's Bohr-Fermi machinery to the leptonic-nucleus regime. **Framework-native: BF Dirac × $(1+a_e)(1+a_\mu)$ Schwinger $= 4464.1905$ MHz vs Liu 1999 $4463.302765(53)$ MHz, residual $+0.8877$ MHz / $+199$ ppm.** Outside the sub-100 ppm bears-fruit threshold but **the cleanest LS-8a multi-loop isolation in the catalogue**: leptonic point-nucleus (antimuon) means residual is purely $\alpha^2(Z\alpha)$ multi-loop QED + cross-register recoil NLO + hadronic VP — no QCD nuclear-structure budget interfering (no Zemach, no polarizability, no FNS). Karshenboim 2005 itemized total of corrections ($+4.703$ MHz, $\sim+1054$ ppm relative to BF strict) cleanly closes agreement to $<1$ ppm: $\alpha^2(Z\alpha) \sim +0.17$ MHz (two-loop QED), $\alpha(Z\alpha)^2(m/M)^2 \sim +0.7$ MHz (recoil + QED), hadronic VP $\sim +0.2$ MHz, plus the dominant Schwinger one-loop already captured by the framework. **Mass-hierarchy ⊗ Layer-2-content matrix:** seven catalogue systems now span both axes — H 21cm (m_e≪m_p, QCD), μH Lamb (overlap, QCD), μH HFS (overlap, QCD), Mu 1S-2S (m_e≪m_μ, no-QCD), Mu Lamb (m_e≪m_μ, no-QCD), Ps HFS (equal-mass, no-QCD), D HFS (m_e≪m_d, QCD I=1), **Mu HFS (m_e≪m_μ, no-QCD HFS — only entry in the dominant m_l≪m_n class with no QCD budget, hence cleanest LS-8a isolation**). The +199 ppm is therefore the empirical depth of the LS-8a wall at $\alpha^2(Z\alpha)$ for Bohr-Fermi-class observables in clean isolation; the wall sits below leading-order precision in this regime (i.e., one-loop QED almost gets us there, with the structural overshoot from the doubled $(1+a_e)(1+a_\mu)$ Schwinger pattern unique to leptonic-nucleus systems). Architecture: Sprint MH Track B BF formula $A_\text{hf} = (2/3) g_e g_\mu \alpha^2 Z^3 m_\text{red}^3 / (m_e m_\mu)$ with $m_\text{red}(e\mu^+) = 0.99519 m_e$, no Zemach (point-lepton magnetization), no cross-register recoil at leading order (already captured in $m_\text{red}^3$). Paper 34 §V gained one machine-precision row (Mu 1S HFS at +199 ppm); §V.B gained one off-precision row (cumulative chain at <1 ppm with Karshenboim Layer-2 itemization). Paper 36 §VIII gained `\subsection{sec:muonium_triple_closure}` documenting the muonium triple closure with mass-hierarchy ⊗ Layer-2-content matrix (~80 lines). - **Precision catalogue extension — Deuterium 1S HFS (post-MH continuation, 2026-05-08):** extends the multi-focal precision arc to the I=1 nuclear-spin axis, complementing Sprint MH (e/μ swap at unchanged proton) and Track 1 Mu/Ps (μ/p swap at unchanged electron, equal-mass limit) by varying nuclear spin with everything else held fixed. **Bohr-Fermi strict prediction lands at +40 ppm** vs Wineland-Ramsey 1972 $\nu_\text{HFS}(D, 1S) = 327.384352522(2)$ MHz — the cleanest framework-native verification of the I=1 cross-register angular coupling structure in the catalogue. **Convention key (the only subtle point):** the atomic-physics Hamiltonian convention uses $g_N = 2 \mu_N/\mu_N^\text{unit}$ independent of I (matches CODATA $g_p = 5.586$ for proton at $2I=1$), giving $g_d^\text{atomic} = 2 \times 0.857 = 1.715$ (differs from CODATA's $g_d = 0.857$ by the factor $2I = 2$). The (2I+1)/2 = 3/2 multiplicity factor between F=3/2 and F=1/2 levels is Clebsch-Gordan, NOT a new mechanism. **Multi-focal architecture verdict at I=1: leading_order_I_independent.** The Fermi-contact Hamiltonian $A_\text{hf} \hat{I} \cdot \hat{S} \delta^3(r)$ is operator-identical for I=1/2 and I=1; Roothaan multipole termination at $L_\text{max} = 2 \ell_\text{max}$ is angular content, not nuclear-spin content. The deuteron's nonzero electric quadrupole moment $Q_d = 0.286$ efm² couples only to gradients (negligible for s-states). **Framework-native chain:** BF strict (327.40 MHz, +40 ppm) → BF + recoil (327.13, -777 ppm) → +Schwinger $a_e$ (327.51, +384 ppm) → +leading Zemach with $r_Z(D) = 2.593$ fm Friar-Payne 2005 (327.48, **+286 ppm**). Operator-level Zemach via `geovac.magnetization_density.hydrogen_zemach_eides_leading_order` matches analytic $-2 Z m_e r_Z$ Eides leading-order to $10^{-14}$ ppm; profile (Gaussian vs exponential) independence preserved. Cumulative residual +286 ppm sits inside the budgeted **W2a + W3 walls**: deuteron polarizability ~+44 ppm (Pachucki-Yerokhin 2010, QCD-internal NN dynamics — W3 inner-factor calibration), multi-loop QED ~few ppm (LS-8a wall), recoil NLO + finite-size charge ~few ppm (Layer-2 input). **Coverage matrix completes:** the e/μ/p mass-hierarchy axis (lepton mass, nuclear mass, equal-mass) AND the I=1/2 vs I=1 nuclear-spin axis are both now empirically verified at sub-100 ppm on framework-native parts across six precision systems (H 21cm, μH Lamb, μH HFS, Mu 1S-2S, Ps HFS, D 1S HFS). Paper 34 §V gained one machine-precision row (BF strict at +40 ppm); §V.B gained one off-precision row (cumulative chain at +286 ppm with structural attribution). Paper 23 §VII gained `\subsection{Test on deuterium 1S hyperfine structure}` documenting the I=1 cross-register validation, with new bibliography entries for Wineland-Ramsey 1972, Friar-Payne 2005, Pachucki-Yerokhin 2010. Files: `debug/precision_catalogue_deuterium_hfs.py`, `debug/precision_catalogue_deuterium_hfs_memo.md`, `debug/data/precision_catalogue_deuterium_hfs.json`.

- **Precision catalogue extension — He $2{}^3P$ fine structure (post-Phillips-Kleinman, 2026-05-08):** first **multi-electron** precision test in the catalogue, opening the *internal multi-focal* axis (two electrons on the same nucleus at structurally distinct effective Z) complementary to the cross-register multi-focal axis (electron $+$ leptonic/nuclear register, Sprint MH / Track 1 / Mu HFS / D HFS). **Framework reproduces $2{}^3P_0$-$2{}^3P_1$ at $-0.014\%$ ($+29{,}612.91$ vs NIST $+29{,}616.951(6)$ MHz) and the $2{}^3P_0$-$2{}^3P_2$ span at $-0.20\%$ ($+31{,}844.07$ vs NIST $+31{,}908.131(6)$ MHz)** via Drake's Breit-Pauli decomposition (Sprint 3 BF-D Drake combining $(\tfrac{3}{50},-\tfrac{2}{5},\tfrac{3}{2},-1)$ + Sprint 4 DD sympy-exact J-pattern from rank-$k$ 6j algebra + Sprint 5 CP/DV bipolar harmonic structure). The small interval $2{}^3P_1$-$2{}^3P_2$ at $+2{,}231.16$ MHz vs NIST $+2{,}291.176(15)$ MHz is at $-2.62\%$ — partial-cancellation amplification of an absolute residual ($-60$ MHz) that sits inside the LS-8a $\alpha^3/\pi$ one-loop QED budget on the absolute scale (the structural cancellation SO ($-58$ GHz) $+$ SS ($-9.5$ GHz) $+$ SOO ($+70$ GHz) $\approx +2.2$ GHz amplifies the fractional error by $\sim10\times$ over the dominant intervals). **Multi-electron internal multi-focal architecture verified:** distinct effective Z's ($Z_\text{eff}(1s)=2$, $Z_\text{eff}(2p)=1$ full-shield) coexist sympy-exactly with their respective Pochhammer rationals; bipolar harmonic decomposition $(k_1{=}0,k_2{=}2)$ direct + $(k_1{=}1,k_2{=}1)$ exchange is angular-content-only (Gaunt-driven), independent of focal-length ratio; Drake combining coefficients are pure rationals (Paper 18 intrinsic tier). **Coverage matrix at seven systems sub-percent on framework-native parts:** mass hierarchy (H, μH, Mu, Ps), nuclear spin (I=1/2, I=1), and now multi-focal kind (cross-register $+$ internal). - **Sprint MH — Muonic hydrogen via the rest-mass projection (2026-05-08):** two-track first application of the multi-focal-composition machinery (Phase C closure) to the precision frontier of bound-state QED. **Track A (2S–2P Lamb shift):** framework reproduces the CREMA 2010 measurement of $\Delta E^{\mu p}_\text{Lamb} = 202.3706(23)$ meV at $-0.10\%$ residual (framework + literature inputs $202.17$ meV vs experimental $202.37$ meV). **Headline architectural innovation:** the Paper 36 contact-form Uehling formula overshoots the muonic regime by $\sim 3.55\times$ because $\beta = 2 m_e a_\mu = 1.475$ (vs $274$ for $ep$) places muonic Bohr scale and electron Compton wavelength in overlap. Replacement is full numerical integration of the Uehling kernel against muonic 2S, 2P wavefunctions, yielding $\Delta E^{\mu p}_\text{VP} = +205.0074$ meV — **matches Antognini 2013 / Pachucki 1996 to $<1$ ppm.** Framework-native subtotal $200.50$ meV; the $+1.67$ meV literature input covers exactly the contributions blocked by the LS-8a renormalization wall (Källén–Sabry two-loop VP, multi-loop QED, recoil NLO) plus QCD-internal nuclear polarizability — precisely as Sprint H1 / Sprint LS-8a / multi-focal-wall pattern predicts. Self-energy gap (24% of value, $0.16$ meV absolute) is leading-order $m_\text{red}$ scaling; Friar moment leading-order at $4.3\%$. Files: `debug/sprint_mh_track_a.py`, `debug/sprint_mh_track_a_memo.md`, `debug/data/sprint_mh_track_a.json`. **Track B (1S Bohr–Fermi hyperfine):** $\nu_F(\mu p) = 182.4433$ meV vs Eides QED-only $182.443$ meV at **$+2$ ppm** with no fits, no muon-specific code path — single rest-mass swap on the same architecture that closed Sprint HF on electronic 21 cm. Mass-scaling ratio $\nu_F(\mu p)/\nu_F(ep) = 31{,}092$ matches the analytic check to $2 \times 10^{-16}$. Zemach mass-enhancement reproduces the Eides muonic target $-7300$ ppm at **0.55%** (manual scaling); enhancement factor $185.94 = m_\text{red}(\mu p)/m_\text{red}(ep)$ exact. Full-theory hyperfine is at $-7710$ ppm vs Krauth $182.725$ meV — same LS-8a wall in the muonic regime (electron-VP / Uehling in muonic potential, $\sim +1.5$ meV, dominant correction). Framework-native pieces (Bohr–Fermi at $+2$ ppm, full Uehling at $<1$ ppm, leading Zemach at $0.55\%$, leading Friar at $4.3\%$) are the parts the framework is supposed to handle; the LS-8a wall (multi-loop QED) is the part it isn't, and the residuals attribute exactly there. Convergence plateaued (n_max=9,10,11 within ±0.06%/step). Three structural findings: (i) **splitting is *less* accurate than absolute energies** — splitting/state error ratio ~34× (12% on splitting vs 2.7–2.8% on individual states); errors on 2³S and 2¹S have *opposite* phase impact, NO common-mode cancellation. (ii) **Variational bound violated for both excited states** (not for 1¹S): graph κ=−1/16 adjacency adds constant inter-shell coupling regardless of orbital extent, overbinding loosely-bound Rydberg-like states. Same mechanism as the small-Z graph-validity-boundary artifact (Z_c≈1.84). (b) `casimir_ci.compute_he_spectrum`'s naive sort-by-energy in M_L=0 sector mislabels excited states for n_max≥3: the second M_L=0 singlet eigenvalue at n_max=3 is dominantly (1s,3p) ¹P, not (1s,2s) ¹S; ss-only sub-block is the clean isolation, used by the sprint as workaround. Catalogue now has nine systems across the mass-hierarchy × nuclear-spin × multi-focal-kind × observable-type axes. Pattern crystallized: **framework reproduces fine structure (Z-scaling clean), hyperfine (|ψ(0)|² is exact), Lamb shift one-loop QED (Dirac-S³ faithful), and rest-mass projections at varied nucleus mass; does NOT reproduce excited-state correlation in single-exponent bases** — graph-native CI is non-variational for atomic Rydberg-like excited states. Multi-exponent atomic split-Z extension (composed-architecture analog for atomic excited states) is the natural follow-on track when a precision-correlation observable is next on the agenda.

- **Cleanup sprint — production-code side findings closed (2026-05-08, post-catalogue):** two parallel cleanup tracks closed both side findings the He 2¹S-2³S sprint surfaced. **(T1 `hypergeometric_slater.compute_rk_float` bug — diagnosis wider than initially flagged.)** The "n ≥ 12 broken" symptom was the visible failure mode of a pervasive float-path issue: catastrophic cancellation between O(10²⁵) Laguerre-product terms summing to O(10¹¹) silently degraded accuracy starting at n = 6 (rel err 1e-7 at n=6, 1e-4 at n=8, 0.2 at n=10, fully wrong sign at n ≥ 12). The k ≥ 2 ssss crash was a separate Gaunt-violation issue (negative power in incomplete-gamma kernel for k > l_a + l_b — physically forbidden but no clean error path). Fix: threshold dispatch at n = 4 — n ≤ 4 uses the existing fast pure-float path bit-identically (~240 μs/call, no regression), n ≥ 5 delegates to `compute_rk_algebraic` and casts to float at the end (correct at any n; n=8: 0.54 s uncached, n=12: 6.5 s, n=20: ~1 min, all paid once per unique quartet via existing `_CACHE_FLOAT`). Gaunt-violating quartets now raise informative `ValueError`. 38 new regression tests in `tests/test_hypergeometric_slater.py` cover n=6..20 across ssss/pppp/spsp/mixed quartets, all verified against `compute_rk_exact` ground truth. **Quantitative refresh resolved (2026-05-08 same-day continuation):** the He 2¹S-2³S sprint was re-run from scratch with the fixed evaluator (full n_max=2..11 sweep, ~30 min wall time, n_max=11 alone 988s `t_build`). **Trajectory is bit-identical to the original at displayed 0.1 cm⁻¹ precision**; largest shift across all n_max is **0.05 cm⁻¹**, two orders of magnitude smaller than the cleanup-sprint worst-case estimate of 10-30 cm⁻¹ and four orders of magnitude smaller than the +762 cm⁻¹ structural residual. The +11.863% verdict at n_max=11 stands; Paper 34 §V.B row gained an annotation but kept the +11.86% number unchanged. **Why the bug had minimal numerical impact on this observable:** the catastrophic-cancellation regime hits *same-shell large-n* integrals hardest, while the He 2¹S-2³S splitting is dominated by exchange integrals K(1s, ns) with at least one small-n index where the cancellation regime is much milder. Additionally, numerical noise in the integrals is *correlated* between singlet and triplet sectors (same orbital configurations, different spin coupling) and partially cancels in the splitting itself. Absolute energies E(2³S) and E(2¹S) (both ~2.7% error) are slightly more sensitive to high-n noise than the splitting (11.9% error), but the dominant residual in all three is the κ-induced excited-state non-variationality, not integral precision. Variational violation, anti-cancellation, structural finding all preserved. Memo §3.1 added documenting the refresh; JSON regenerated; log at `debug/data/he_refresh.log`. **Net cleanup: both side findings (T1 and T2) are closed and the quantitative refresh confirms the catalogue conclusion stands.** **(T2 `casimir_ci.compute_he_spectrum` state-labeling — promoted ss-only sub-block from sprint workaround to production API.)** New kwarg `subblock: Optional[Tuple[int, int]] = None` on both `build_graph_native_fci` and `compute_he_spectrum`; default `None` preserves existing behavior bit-identically (verified by 4 backward-compat regression tests at n_max=2,3,4); `subblock=(0,0)` gives clean ¹S/³S, `(0,1)` gives ¹P/³P, etc. Order-invariant (sorting before comparison). Docstrings updated to document the M_L-mixing problem at n_max ≥ 3 and recommend the right kwarg. 24 new tests in `tests/test_casimir_ci.py` cover backward-compat, ss-only at n_max=3,4,5 (reproduces sprint memo §3 reference at n_max=5: 7308.7713 cm⁻¹, matching to 0.01 cm⁻¹), sp sub-block, edge cases (negative-l raises ValueError, empty shells, Hermiticity, Hund ordering). All 21 production call sites verified backward-compatible — no caller updates needed. **Net status:** both side findings closed; combined test verification 122/122 pass + 9 slow skipped (`pytest tests/test_hypergeometric_slater.py tests/test_casimir_ci.py -x`). CLAUDE.md §12 Slater F^k row updated with corrected accuracy claims and new threshold-dispatch architecture. Files: `geovac/hypergeometric_slater.py` (+~155 lines threshold dispatch + private mpmath helper), `tests/test_hypergeometric_slater.py` (new, 38 tests), `geovac/casimir_ci.py` (+~80 lines subblock kwarg), `tests/test_casimir_ci.py` (+~280 lines, 24 new tests).

- **Paper 34 sixteenth projection — two-body Dirac / Breit retardation (2026-05-08, PI authorization):** Added the 16th projection to Paper 34's inventory motivated by the Ps 1S-2S sprint's structural finding (sixth and cleanest multi-focal-composition wall instance; sprint memo §6 had flagged this for PI review on 2026-05-08, PI authorized the addition). **Structural content:** variable m_l/m_n (rest-mass ratio that does NOT vanish in the equal-mass limit, distinguishing this from rest-mass projection), dimension energy, transcendental α⁴·ℚ, Layer 1→2 (Layer-2 input similar to magnetization-density / Zemach). Mechanism: takes the framework's single-particle Eides §3.2 SE Lamb-shift bracket → full two-body Breit Hamiltonian for the bound state. Empirical anchor: Ps 1S-2S framework-native at +64.75 ppm vs Fee 1993 (one data point so far, honestly flagged in §III.16 entry); Layer-2 α⁴ Breit input from Penin-Pivovarov 1998 (PRL 80, 2101) closes the residual to sub-MHz at the ~80 GHz scale. Distinct from rest-mass projection (which preserves the transcendental ring under m_red rescaling — this projection is also α⁴·ℚ ring-preserving but via two-body kinematics rather than mass rescaling of single-particle observables), distinct from spectral action / Sturmian (single-particle, fundamentally one-electron), distinct from magnetization-density (which couples to nuclear spatial structure; this is a relativistic kinematic effect at the leading α⁴ order). **Headline structural finding from the §VII audit:** the (rest_mass, breit_retardation) pair is **the first one-way composition pair in the dictionary driven by variable-refinement dependence rather than Layer transition**. Both projections output to Layer 2 (rest-mass 1→2, Breit 2→2), but Breit's variable m_l/m_n is a ratio of two species' rest-masses that the rest-mass projection itself introduces. The reverse order would require the ratio to be defined before the masses exist. This is structurally distinct from Drake-Swainson's existing one-way cells (which are Layer-driven) and from the hopf+spinor non-commutation in T2 (which is bundle-non-trivial composition). Real new content from doing the audit, not a forced consequence of it. **§VII T3 composition table** expanded 15×15 → 16×16 = 256 cells: approximate counts ~196 commute (76.6%), ~26 one-way pairs (+4 in P_16 row/column), 6 variable conflicts (unchanged — m_l/m_n is novel), 4 idempotent (Sturmian + Wigner 3j + Drake-Swainson + Breit retardation), 3 inverse pairs. Cell counts marked approximate (~) — exact recomputation against `debug/data/tx_a_composition_table.json` deferred to a follow-on TX-A-style audit. Drake-Swainson's prior status as the unique 2→2 idempotent retired (now two such projections). Edits applied to `papers/group6_precision_observations/paper_34_projection_taxonomy.tex`: abstract count thirteen→sixteen; §II preamble narrative; §III.16 new subsection (~62 lines, structural entry with Source/Target/Variables/Dimension/Transcendental/Used in/Empirical anchor/Honest scope/Structural reading subsections); §IV three-axis dictionary table new row; §IV V/D-correlation Observation extended (8/8 → 9/9); §V.B Ps 1S-2S row gained cross-reference to §III.16; §VII T2 weak-minimality narrative now flags TWO non-commuting pairs distinguishing variable-refinement (rest_mass × Breit) from bundle-non-trivial (hopf × spinor lift); §VII T3 expanded with documented commutation determinations; §VIII Open Questions and §IX Conclusion updated. **Side benefit:** caught and fixed a pre-existing LaTeX bug — Paper 34 had `\begin{theorem}` blocks but `\newtheorem{theorem}{Theorem}` was not declared. New module `geovac/screened_valence_basis.py` (~280 lines, 25 fast tests passing) provides `screened_valence_eigenvalue(Z_nuc, block_n, l, n_val_offset)` and `apply_screened_valence_correction()`. Wired into `build_balanced_hamiltonian` via `screened_valence_basis: bool = False` kwarg with bit-exact backward compat preserved (LiH 878 Pauli regression bit-identical at machine precision). **Eigenvalue substitution verified to literature**: Na 3s = -0.170 Ha (CR67 single-zeta), Na 4s = -0.067 Ha, Na 4p = -0.051 Ha — all physically bound, sign and magnitude consistent with Clementi-Roetti HF tabulation. h1 diagonal correction is a +0.611 Ha trace shift on the NaH valence (3s + 4s + 3·4p), large compared to descent depth (0.357 Ha after W1c). **8-configuration NaH PES at max_n=2 (Q=20, 2e FCI)**: all 8 still monotonically descending, NO internal equilibrium minimum. R_min = 2.5 (smallest tested) for every config. Descent-depth ladder: bare 6.244 → +W1c 0.357 (17.5×) → +W1c+PK 0.305 (1.17× addl) → +W1c+PK+SV 0.313 (0.97× addl, slight worsening). The screened-valence diagonal correction does NOT close the wall. **Critical structural finding (the substantive result)**: the SV correction is **R-independent at the diagonal h1 level** — eigenvalues are properties of the on-center potential, not of the bond. The screened correction matrix is bit-identical at R=2.5 and R=10 (max abs diff 5.55×10⁻¹⁷). A constant diagonal h1 shift cannot affect the descent-depth (an R-dependent energy difference). The named target ("replace Z_orb=1 hydrogenic Na valence basis with screened Schrödinger eigenstates") is **incomplete as named** — it requires wavefunction-shape substitution in cross-V_ne and within-block ERIs, not just diagonal h1 substitution. **Diagnostic experiment (debug/w1c_residual_nah_track3_diag.py)**: testing the cross-V_ne integral with hydrogenic-shape labels at the *physical* n (block_n=1, l=0 → n_phys=3 hydrogenic 3s instead of 1s) shows that the framework over-attracts by 0.81 Ha at R=2.5 vs the physical-n shape, and by only 0.14 Ha at R=10. **Differential -0.674 Ha** — about **1.9× larger than the W1c-residual descent (0.357 Ha)**. Structural reading: a wavefunction-shape substitution would over-correct from the current attraction profile and **likely produce a binding minimum**. The genuine residual lives in cross-V_ne integration shape, not diagonal eigenvalue. The hydrogenic Z=1 1s on Na has mean radius 1.50 bohr; the actual Na 3s screened wavefunction has mean radius 4.47 bohr — opposite shape biases at the orbital extent level. **Verdict**: the SV diagonal correction is necessary architectural infrastructure (wired and tested) but not sufficient for binding. Next named engineering closure is **wavefunction-shape substitution in cross-center V_ne and within-block ERIs**, not strict-Schmidt orthogonalization. Strict-Schmidt remains the mathematically definitive but expensive alternative; the diagnostic suggests the cheaper "physical-n hydrogenic relabeling" of the Na valence states would close most of the wall and is a 1-week sprint, not multi-week. **Pattern crystallization**: the diagnostic-before-engineering rule (memory `feedback_diagnostic_before_engineering.md`, 2026-05-08) applies inside this sprint. Two engineering attempts (PK cross-center + screened-valence diagonal) have now landed clean modules but failed to close binding; the third pre-implementation diagnostic (cross-V_ne shape sweep) shows the genuine target is in cross-V_ne shape, not diagonal h1. Files: `geovac/screened_valence_basis.py`, `tests/test_balanced_coupled_screened_valence.py` (25 tests), `debug/w1c_residual_nah_track3.py` (8-config PES driver), `debug/w1c_residual_nah_track3_diag.py` (diagnostic), `debug/data/w1c_residual_nah_track3_results.json`, `debug/data/w1c_residual_nah_track3_diag.json`, `debug/w1c_residual_nah_track3_memo.md` (~3500 words). - **Paper 40 arc — Unified GH-convergence on compact Lie groups (2026-05-15 / 2026-05-16):** ten-sprint arc closing the math.OA propinquity triptych (Papers 38, 39, 40). Generalizes Paper 38's SU(2) propinquity convergence theorem to **all compact connected Lie groups with bi-invariant metric**, with the headline structural finding that **the rate constant 4/π is universal across the class** (independent of rank, Weyl group order, Lie-type). Companion to Gaudillot-Estrada–vS 2025 (IMRN 2025, Issue 13, paper rnaf197; arXiv:2310.14733), which proved state-space GH at the same generality without rate and without Dirac. **Sequence of sprints:** (1) **Track 1 scoping** identified Class 1 (compact Lie groups, bi-invariant metric) as the right abstraction; literature audit found Gaudillot-Estrada–vS as the natural precedent. (2) **Sprint P-A Casimir-triangle FALSE:** the literal "Casimir triangle inequality" |C(π)−C(π')|≤C(σ) is false even at SU(2) (j=1, j'=1/2 counterexample); Paper 38's L3 actually uses the Dirac-triangle inequality |D(π)−D(π')|≤√C(σ) per direct reading of `debug/r25_l3_proof_memo.md`. (3) **SU(3) Dirac-triangle verification** (PM-direct, no agent): 100/100 panel pairs pass with max ratio 0.672, asymptote→1⁻. (4) **Sprint Q-rate** extracted c(SU(3))≈1.243 with 12/π² vs 4/π ambiguous. (5) **Sprint Sp(2)/G₂ rate-constant test** decisively resolved A vs B: Sp(2) extracted 1.087 (14.6% off A, 33% off B), G₂ extracted 1.177 (7.6% off A, 51.6% off B). **Conjecture B (Weyl-formula c=2|W|/π^r) decisively falsified at G₂ 91% gap; rank-invariant c=4/π wins.** (6) **Sprint L3-proof** at SU(3)/SU(4)/Sp(2)/G₂: 977/977 numerical pass at exact rational arithmetic; trivial-case + Cartan-product proofs rigorous; named gap on interior summands. SIDE FINDING: Sprint MR-C's published 80-digit string was wrong from digit 12+ (float-precision panel-point contamination); CLAUDE.md §2 + MR-C memo errata applied. (8) **Sprint L3-analytic-complete: PROVED-WITH-NAMED-GAP.** PRV-summand theorem at all ranks via Kumar (1988) + Vinberg (1990): for every w∈W, σ_w=dominant image of λ+wλ'* is a summand of π⊗π'* and |σ_w+ρ|²≥|λ−λ'+ρ|². Covers asymptotic family (n,0,…,0)⊗(1,0,…,0)*, rigorously establishing **C₃(G)=1 asymptotic-tight at all ranks** in all simple Lie algebra types (A_n, B_n, C_n, D_n, G₂, F₄, E₆, E₇, E₈). (9) **Sprint L2-universal-proof: PROVED-AT-ALL-RANKS** at Paper 38 Appendix A rigor. **Plancherel × Vandermonde cancellation theorem:** in the dual-Coxeter normalization, the Plancherel weight √(dim V_π) from the central spectral Fejér kernel exactly cancels the Vandermonde Jacobian |Δ(t)|² from the Weyl integration formula (both have the same ∏_{α>0} product structure). All rank-, |W|-, N_+-dependence drops out at leading order, leaving the pure 1D Stein-Weiss constant 4/π from each positive-root direction's Euler-Catalan asymptote ∑_{d odd} 1/d² = π²/8. Three-step proof: closed-form sum-rule → rank-1 reduction via Pfaff-Watson/Weyl character formula → universal cancellation. - **Paper 42 drafted — Tomita-Takesaki modular structure on truncated SU(2) spectral triples (2026-05-16):** standalone math.OA / J. Geom. Phys. style paper consolidating Sprints L0 + L1 + L1-tighten as the fourth math.OA paper in the GeoVac series (after Papers 38, 39, 40). 2088 lines, 11,613 words, 23 pages compiled PDF (587 KB); three-pass clean LaTeX compilation, zero undefined references. 10 sections + 2 appendices, 5 theorems + 4 propositions/corollaries + 2 definitions + 2 remarks, 3 numerical tables, 37 bibliography entries (28 published + 9 internal preprints). **Headline result:** the four-witness Wick-rotation theorem (Hartle-Hawking 1976 + Sewell 1982 + Bisognano-Wichmann 1976 + Unruh 1976) closes at the operator-system level on the truncated Camporesi-Higuchi spectral triple T_{n_max} via two structurally independent but operator-action conjugate constructions — geometric BW-α (K_α = J_polar, integer spectrum, Theorem 5.4 STRONG_IDENTIFICATION) and Tomita-Takesaki BW-γ (K_TT = -log Δ via polar decomposition on GNS Hilbert-Schmidt space, Theorem 6.3 UNIFIED_STRONG). Flow conjugacy σ_t^TT(O) = σ_{-t}^α(O) bit-exact (Theorem 7.1). Six-witness collapse to single operator-system construction at algebra-action level (Corollary 8.1). All verified bit-exactly at n_max ∈ {2,3,4,5}. **Load-bearing scope finding (§7.2):** the unified closure rests on H_local = K_α^W/β; the framework's intrinsic Camporesi-Higuchi Dirac D_W is NOT the right local Hamiltonian for the BW vacuum at β=2π (would give half-integer spectrum and the bit-exact closure would fail). Flagged as derived structural finding, not a uniqueness theorem; spectral-action paradigm (Chamseddine-Connes) and thermal-time paradigm (Connes-Rovelli) point to different generators on the wedge KMS state. Five open questions (O1-O5) named in §10: Lorentzian (3,1) extension; non-tracial wedge states; spectral-action vs modular-Hamiltonian generator distinction; higher-rank compact Lie group extension (Paper 40 generality); cross-manifold modular structures (Paper 24 §V W2b blocker). **Nieuviarts NO-GO documented as honest related-work negative** (§3.2 footnote): twist morphism Def 2.2 of arXiv:2502.18105v3 explicitly restricted to even-dim manifolds, S³ at KO-dim 3 (odd) does not qualify; direct BBB Krein lift remains the path. **Microtype disabled** to avoid MiKTeX font-expansion environmental issue (same fix as Papers 38/39/40). - **Sprint L1-tighten — Load-bearing Tomita-Takesaki BW-γ closure (2026-05-16 evening):** **CLOSED — UNIFIED_STRONG at every tested cutoff and witness.** Same-day continuation of Sprint L1 tightening the BW-α-only closure to a load-bearing Tomita-Takesaki construction. The L1 closure used the geometric BW-α realization K = J_polar as the load-bearing object; the Tomita BW-γ realization was only an expectation-level KMS cross-check. L1-tighten rebuilds BW-γ at the full Tomita-Takesaki level on the GNS Hilbert-Schmidt space H_GNS = M_{dim_W}(ℂ) ≅ ℂ^{dim_W²}: build modular operator Δ via polar decomposition S = J_TT · Δ^{1/2}, extract K_TT = -log Δ, verify σ_{2π}^TT(O) = O at the operator-action level. **Verdict at every n_max ∈ {2, 3, 4, 5} and every witness: UNIFIED_STRONG (PI's prior outcome 1).** Maximum σ_TT(2π) residual: 1.09×10⁻¹⁶ at n_max=2 (dim_GNS=64), 1.07×10⁻¹⁵ at n_max=3 (dim_GNS=400), 3.03×10⁻¹⁵ at n_max=4 (dim_GNS=1600), 4.79×10⁻¹⁵ at n_max=5 (dim_GNS=4900). All at machine precision. **Operator-action conjugacy verified bit-exact:** σ_t^TT(a) = σ_{-t}^α(a) at t=1 with residual <10⁻¹⁶ (the two flows are operator-action-level conjugates; at the period t=2π the sign is invisible because e^{±i·2π·n}=1 for integer n). **J_TT² = +I at the FULL Tomita level:** the state-dependent J_TT(X) = ρ^{1/2}·X*·ρ^{-1/2} satisfies J²=+I to machine precision (the L1 verification only checked the canonical U=I sanity case; L1-tighten verifies the genuine ρ^{1/2}-weighted Tomita conjugation). Categorically distinct from Connes J_GV which has J_GV²=-I (KO-dim 3). **Construction:** natural local Hamiltonian H_local := K_α^W / β makes β·H_local = K_α^W on the wedge with integer spectrum two_m_j, giving the wedge KMS state ρ_W = e^{-K_α^W}/Z (β-independent at the algebra-action level, the operator-system analog of the Wightman BW vacuum ρ_W ∝ e^{-2π·K_boost} on the Rindler wedge). Cross-witness collapse is preserved at the Tomita-Takesaki level — in fact deeper than the BW-α version because ρ_W is itself β-independent, so all six witnesses (BW + HH×2 + Sew + Unruh×2) give bit-identical Δ and K_TT. **Honest scope preserved:** unified closure rests on the BW-aligned local Hamiltonian choice; alternative H_local = D_W (Camporesi-Higuchi Dirac, half-integer spectrum) would not have integer β·H_local and would not close bit-exactly — the framework's intrinsic Dirac is not the right local Hamiltonian for the BW vacuum at β=2π. **Verdict graduation:** the four-witness Wick-rotation theorem is closed at the operator-system level (Riemannian) via **both** the geometric BW-α and the Tomita-Takesaki BW-γ readings, not just one. The L1 §7.3 "BW-α-only" caveat is removed. - **Sprint L2-B — Krein space construction at signature (3, 1) (2026-05-16):** **CLOSED at every tested cutoff.** First concrete deliverable of the Lorentzian-extension arc beyond Sprint L0. All Krein axioms (J² = +I, J* J = I, J* = J, K = K^+ ⊕ K^- with dim K^± = dim K/2) verified bit-exact (Frobenius residual = 0.0 in float64) at every (n_max, N_t) ∈ {1, 2, 3} × {1, 11, 21} panel cell. **Load-bearing Riemannian-limit check passed bit-identically:** at N_t = 1, K reduces to H_GV^{n_max} bit-identically (dimension formula 2/3·n_max·(n_max+1)·(n_max+2) = 4, 16, 40 matches Paper 32 Def 3.2 exactly; basis labels via FullDiracLabel.__eq__ identical object-by-object; J matrix Frobenius residual = 0.0). Bit-exactness follows from J being the Kronecker product of a real {0, 1} permutation matrix and an identity — no transcendentals, no division, no rounding error in IEEE 754. - **Sprint L2-F.1 + Pythagorean extension scoping (2026-05-17):** Two-track post-L2-closure sprint testing whether the Paper 42 §7.2 H_local ≠ D_W structural finding has additional algebraic structure beyond the bit-exact residual values reported by L2-E. **Headline structural result:** on the hemispheric wedge $W_L$ of the Lorentzian Krein space, $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L \rangle_{\mathrm{HS}} = 0$ **bit-exact at every panel cell tested** (n_max ∈ {1,…,6}, all six witnesses, N_t ∈ {1, 11}), with closed-form Hilbert–Schmidt squared distance $r^2(n; \kappa_g) = \kappa_g^2 \cdot S(n)/(4\pi^2) + D(n)$ where $S(n) = n(n+1)(n+2)(2n^2+4n-1)/15$ and $D(n) = n(n+1)(n+2)(2n+1)(2n+3)/20$. The $1/\pi^2$ prefactor on $\|H_{\mathrm{local}}\|^2$ is the **master Mellin engine M1 Hopf-base-measure signature** (same $1/\pi^2$ as the L2 quantitative rate $4/\pi$ and as the Stefan–Boltzmann Matsubara prefactor). PSLQ-verified at 100 dps with coefficient ceiling $10^6$. **Mechanism (subspace decomposition, structural sketch):** $H_{\mathrm{local}} = K_\alpha^W/\beta = J_{\mathrm{polar}}/(2\pi)$ lives in the diagonal subspace of $B(\mathcal{K}_W)$ (in the full-Dirac basis under the BW choice); $D_W^L$ lives in the off-diagonal subspace ($\Delta n = \pm 1$, intertwines $\pm m_j$ chirality partners). Diagonal and off-diagonal operator subspaces are orthogonal under the Hilbert–Schmidt inner product. The Pythagorean relation $r^2 = \|H_{\mathrm{local}}\|^2 + \|D_W^L\|^2$ is then forced. Formal proof of the subspace decomposition (as opposed to PSLQ-verified empirical observation) is the named follow-on. **Track 1 (six-witness universality):** HS-orthogonality verified universal across all six modular witnesses (BW + HH×2 + Sewell + Unruh×2) at 18 panel cells, max $|\langle H, D\rangle| = 8.9 \times 10^{-16}$. Universality is a $\kappa_g$-linearity corollary of the BW result; the closed form above generalises by $\kappa_g$-substitution. Pythagoras $r^2 = \|H\|^2 + \|D\|^2$ verified at every cell. N_t > 1 spot check at (n_max, N_t) = (3, 11) confirms orthogonality persists in the temporal-derivative regime where $D_L = i(\gamma^0 \otimes \partial_t + D_{\mathrm{GV}} \otimes I)$ adds content beyond $D_{\mathrm{GV}}$. **Track 2 (Pythagorean extension scoping):** two candidate extensions of the orthogonality structure beyond Paper 42/43 spectral triples were scoped diagnostically. (a) **SU(2) Wilson lattice gauge on $S^3$** (Paper 30): **GO-WITH-PREREQS.** Trivial-vacuum orthogonality is automatic (the L_1 = B^T B kinetic term lives in a structurally distinct sector from any candidate "local Hamiltonian" on the lattice gauge sector); needs matter-coupling wired into `geovac/su2_wilson_gauge.py` (~1–2 weeks) before the substantive question (survival under Haar averaging at non-trivial $\beta_{\mathrm{Wilson}}$) can be asked. (b) **SU(3) Wilson on $S^5$ Bargmann lattice** (Sprint ST-SU3): **NO-GO**, with four structural obstructions: (i) no spinor sector on the $(N, 0)$ Hardy tower (Paper 24 §III); (ii) no second-order/first-order distinction with separate Dirac (Paper 24 Theorem 3, HO rigidity); (iii) no half-integer wedge — $m_l$ is integer on Bargmann, so the natural modular period is $\pi$ not $2\pi$ and the K spectrum cannot have integer eigenvalues two_m_j; (iv) Coulomb/HO category mismatch resurfaces at the modular-Hamiltonian level — same blocker as G4b cross-manifold (`debug/g4_cross_manifold_scoping_memo.md`) and as Sprint L2 §7.2-class generator distinctions. This establishes the **fourth layer** of the Paper 24 §V Coulomb/HO asymmetry: (i) spectrum-computing role of $L_0$; (ii) calibration $\pi$; (iii) non-abelian Wilson gauge with natural matter coupling; (iv) **modular-Hamiltonian structure of the wedge KMS state** (the Coulomb side admits HS-orthogonality on the Krein wedge with closed-form M1 prefactor; the HO side does not admit the construction at all). **Paper edits applied (5 edits across 4 papers, all three-pass clean):** Paper 43 §10.2 new `subsec:pythagorean_orthogonality` with Corollary `cor:pythagorean_orthogonality` (closed form + structural reading + scope statement on formal-proof follow-on); §11 (Open questions) O4 extended with formal subspace-decomposition proof as named follow-on. Paper 42 §8 new `rem:pythagorean_underlies_collapse` placing the six-witness collapse inside the HS-orthogonality structure; §10 O3 extended with Pythagorean refinement (residual norms ‖H_local − D_W‖_F now have closed-form components, sharpening the open question). Paper 32 §VIII new `rem:pythagorean_m1_closure` connecting the orthogonality $1/\pi^2$ prefactor to the master Mellin engine M1 closure. Paper 24 §V new `subsec:asymmetry_layer4` extending the Coulomb/HO asymmetry from three layers to four (Paper 31 §sec:coulomb_ho cross-reference added). Paper 32 §VIII.C G4b paragraph revised — no longer "fourth layer" since Paper 24 §V now records four layers explicitly; G4b reframed as sibling of the asymmetry-layer-4 obstruction at the cross-manifold setting. Paper 24 had a pre-existing `\newtheorem{theorem}` and `\newtheorem{corollary}` missing-declaration LaTeX bug (caught + fixed in this session with single-line preamble addition between `\usepackage{xcolor}` and `\begin{document}`); no other Paper 24 content changed. Compilation: Papers 42/43/32 three-pass clean zero substantive warnings; Paper 24 three-pass clean after preamble fix. **Honest scope:** orthogonality is **empirically PSLQ-verified at 18 panel cells** with closed-form $r^2$ matching to coefficient ceiling $10^6$; the **subspace-decomposition mechanism is a structural sketch** sufficient to identify the M1 signature and the diagonal/off-diagonal partition; **formal proof of the subspace decomposition** (operator-theoretic, not panel-PSLQ) is the named follow-on (Option 2 from PI's earlier triage). WH1 PROVEN is not re-opened; this sprint refines L2-E's H_local ≠ D_W finding with additional algebraic structure but does not change the Paper 42 §10 O3 open-question status. The fourth Coulomb/HO asymmetry layer is genuinely new structural content; Paper 31 §sec:coulomb_ho three-layer count is now formally extended to four with explicit citation to this sprint. **Bit-exactness rule of thumb (PI-adopted heuristic, recorded as feedback memory):** "bit-exact closure = green light (we're operating on the skeleton); residuals = caution light (Layer 2 work); neither = drift detector needed." The rule organises sprint triage: bit-exact closures (six-witness collapse, σ_{2π}=1, J²=±I, HS-orthogonality) are skeleton operations and warrant publication-grade follow-through; residuals at machine-precision-but-not-zero (e.g. L1 σ_{2π} residual scaling as O(√dim_H · ε_machine)) live at the Layer-2 boundary; results that are neither bit-exact nor machine-precision-bounded warrant a drift-detector diagnostic before further engineering. Used productively across L2-F.1, the six-witness probe, and the SU(2)/SU(3) scoping sprints. - **Sprint L3b-2 + Paper 45 — K⁺-restricted weak-form Lorentzian propinquity convergence theorem (2026-05-18):** **CLOSED — main theorem proved in four sub-sprints on the L3b foundation laid down in v2.46.0.** Single-day sprint closing the convergence-theorem leg of the Lorentzian-extension program for truncated GeoVac spectral triples. To our knowledge the **first published Lorentzian propinquity convergence theorem on truncated Krein spectral triples in the math.OA literature**; concurrent-work audit run during pre-submission hardening returned CLEAR. **Main theorem:** on truncated SU(2) × U(1)_T Krein spectral triples with $\Krein_{\nmax, \Nt} = \HGV^{\nmax} \otimes \C^{\Nt}$, $\JL = \JL^{\spat} \otimes I_{\Nt}$ at BBB $(m, n) = (4, 6)$ Peskin-Schroeder chiral basis, $\DL = i(\gamma^{0} \otimes \partial_{t} + \DGV \otimes I_{\Nt})$ per van den Dungen 2016 Proposition 4.1, $\Lprop(\Tcal^{L}_{\nmax,\Nt,T}, \Tcal^{L}_{\Manifold}) \le C_{3}^{\mathrm{joint}} \cdot \gamma^{\mathrm{joint}}_{\nmax, \Nt, T} \to 0$ where $\Lprop$ is the **K⁺-restricted weak-form Lorentzian propinquity** $\Lprop(\Tcal_{1}^{L}, \Tcal_{2}^{L}) := \Lambda(\Tcal_{1}^{+}, \Tcal_{2}^{+})$ on the Krein-positive Hilbert-space restriction $\Kplus = \{|\psi\rangle : \JL|\psi\rangle = +|\psi\rangle\}$ where the Krein product reduces to a positive-definite Hilbert inner product and Latrémolière 2017/2023 machinery applies verbatim, $C_{3}^{\mathrm{joint}} \le 1$ asymptotically tight (inherited from Paper 38 L3 via the joint Lichnerowicz structural identity), and $\gamma^{\mathrm{joint}}_{\nmax, \Nt, T} = O(\log\nmax/\nmax + T/\Nt)$. **Five-lemma proof transferred from Paper 38 across four sub-sprints.** **(Sub-sprint A — joint Lichnerowicz / L3, PROVED.)** Structural identity $[\DL, a_{s} \otimes a_{t}] = i[\DGV, a_{s}] \otimes a_{t}$ — the time-chirality cross term $\{\gamma^{0}, \DGV\} = 0$ on the chirality-doubled basis (since $\gamma^{0}$ anticommutes with $\DGV$ as a Cl(3, 1) gamma matrix and $\DGV$ is chirality-diagonal), so the temporal direction contributes **nothing** to the joint commutator and the joint $C_{3}^{\mathrm{joint}} = C_{3}^{\SU(2)}$ verbatim — an unexpected structural simplification. **(Sub-sprint B — joint cb-norm / L2, PROVED.)** Joint central spectral Fejér kernel $\Kjoint = \KSU_{\nmax} \otimes \KU_{\Nt, T}$ on $\SU(2) \times \Uone$ with factorised Plancherel symbol; Bożejko-Fendler central-multiplier equality on the amenable compact group product gives joint cb-norm $\cbnorm{S_{\Kjoint}} = 2/(\nmax + 1)$ — **$\Nt$-independent**, a second unexpected simplification reflecting the trivial Plancherel structure of $\Uone$. Factorisation exact in sympy rationals. **(Sub-sprint C — joint Berezin reconstruction / L4, PROVED.)** Tensor-product Berezin map $\Bjoint = B^{\SU(2)} \otimes B^{\Uone}$ inherits the four required properties (positivity, contractivity, approximate identity with rate $\gamma^{\mathrm{joint}} = O(\log\nmax/\nmax + T/\Nt)$, L3 compatibility) factor-by-factor; PURE_TENSOR structure means no cross-factor verification needed. **(Sub-sprint D — K⁺-weak-form propinquity / L5, PROVED-WITH-NAMED-GAP.)** Latrémolière tunneling pair $(\Bjoint, \Pjoint)$ assembled on the K⁺ Hilbert-space restriction; reach and height contributions bounded factor-wise; main theorem follows. **Named gap:** Latrémolière 2017 §5 K⁺-preservation bookkeeping is sketched analytically but not closed in full detail — given the trivial-multiplier K⁺-preservation already established at L3a-1 (Paper 44, v2.46.0), this is bookkeeping rather than an analytical obstruction. **Numerical verification panel:** $\Lprop$ values at $(\nmax, \Nt) \in \{(2, 3), (3, 5), (4, 7)\} = \{2.0746, 1.6101, 1.3223\}$, bit-identical to Paper 38/39's Riemannian SU(2) bound at matching $\nmax$; convergence ratio $\Lprop(4, 7) / \Lprop(2, 3) = 0.6374$ matches Paper 38/39 bit-exactly. Temporal direction expands the multiplier algebra (admissible $a_t$ grows with $\Nt$) but does not tighten the Lipschitz-height bound — $\Nt$-dependence lives in reach (γ-moment), not height (cb-norm), per Sub-sprint B's $\Nt$-independent cb-norm. **Riemannian-limit recovery at $\Nt = 1$ bit-exact** — joint construction reduces to Paper 38's single-factor bound bit-exactly because $\Bjoint|_{\Nt = 1} = B^{\SU(2)} \otimes B^{\Uone}_{1, T} = B^{\SU(2)}$ (the $\Nt = 1$ temporal Berezin map is identity on the single Fourier mode). **Paper 45 drafted and pre-submission hardened to ARXIV_READY status:** seventh math.OA standalone in the GeoVac series (siblings 38, 39, 40, 42, 43, 44) at `papers/group1_operator_algebras/paper_45_lorentzian_propinquity.tex` (1,721 lines, 8,088 words, 18 pages, three-pass clean LaTeX, 33 bibitems). Pre-submission hardening pass applied **5 mechanical citation fixes** (arXiv:2601.22171 author vdD → de Groot; arXiv:2510.13069 authors Mondino-Sämann → Che/Perales/Sormani; Nieuviarts initial corrected to G.; Bożejko-Fendler bibitem alignment; Latrémolière 2018 not 2017) — bibliography fidelity fixes, no substantive content changes. **Concurrent-work re-check during hardening: CLEAR** — no published Lorentzian Latrémolière-style propinquity exists as of May 2026 (verified across Latrémolière 2017/2023/2025, Hekkelman-McDonald 2024a/b, Toyota 2023, Farsi-Latrémolière 2024/2025, Leimbach-vS 2024, all strictly Riemannian; Mondino-Sämann 2022–2025 synthetic Lorentzian GH program is categorically different — pre-length spaces with causal diamonds, not operator-algebraic spectral triples). **Test verification:** 316 tests pass across L3a-1 + L3b foundation + L3b-2 spot-checks (118 fast + 3 slow from v2.46.0 + new spot-checks verifying joint Plancherel factorisation and $\Nt = 1$ Riemannian-limit recovery), zero regression on any upstream baseline. **Three structural simplifications crystallised as substantive new content** (unexpected ahead of the sprint, recorded honestly): (i) PURE_TENSOR structure of the propinquity tunneling pair (L4 factorises with no cross-factor work); (ii) vanishing time-chirality cross-term $\{\gamma^{0}, \DGV\} = 0$ (L3 joint Lichnerowicz = spatial Lichnerowicz); (iii) $\Nt$-independent joint cb-norm (L2 reflects trivial central-multiplier structure of $\Uone$). The three together mean temporal compactification does not generate new analytical obstructions beyond what the foundation already handled. **Honest scope (preserved consistently):** (i) K⁺-weak-form only — strong-form Lorentzian propinquity (Latrémolière-style metric on Krein-signature spectral triples in their own right, without K⁺ restriction) **remains an open NCG-math problem named as Q1** (Paper 45 §1.4 G1), requiring an indefinite-inner-product analog of the operator-norm Lipschitz seminorm; (ii) compact temporal radius $T$ canonical (BW modular period $T = 2\pi$); de-compactification $T \to \infty$ is a separate program (Sprint L3c, named gap G2); (iii) cross-manifold $\Tcal_{\sthree} \otimes \Tcal_{\mathrm{Hardy}(S^5)}$ blocked at NCG-framework level by Paper 24 §V four-layer Coulomb/HO asymmetry (named gap G3); (iv) inner-factor calibration data (Higgs / Yukawa selection) orthogonal to the present convergence theorem (named gap G4). **WH1 PROVEN status maintained** — the Lorentzian convergence result is structurally additive on top of the proven Riemannian foundation (Paper 38), not a re-test of it. Built from sprint memos: `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_A_lichnerowicz_memo.md` (joint L3), `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_B_cb_norm_memo.md` (joint L2), `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_C_berezin_memo.md` (joint L4), `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_D_propinquity_memo.md` (joint L5), `debug/l3b_2_preflight_concurrent_work_memo.md` (related-work hardening), `debug/l3b_first_move_memo.md` (foundation, v2.46.0), `debug/l3a_1_lorentzian_operator_system_memo.md` (L1' / Paper 44). No production `geovac/` modifications (L3b foundation modules from v2.46.0 are sufficient substrate). No `tests/` modifications beyond spot-check additions. Next-direction options surfaced: (A) Sprint L3b-3 numerical-panel sweep via existing K⁺ state-space SDP machinery (~1–2 weeks); (B) Sprint L3c de-compactification scoping (~3–6 weeks); (C) Strong-form Lorentzian propinquity Q1 attack (multi-month NCG-math problem); (D) return to physics-side precision catalogue or state-side dictionary work.

- **Sprint L3b-2a–d — Strong-form Lorentzian propinquity convergence theorem (2026-05-22):** **CLOSED — Paper 45 §1.4 Q1/G1 named open problem proved across four sub-sprints in a single multi-session day.** The strong-form Lorentzian propinquity bound — a Latrémolière-style metric on the FULL Krein space WITHOUT K⁺ restriction (the gap Paper 45 carried forward as the principal open NCG-math problem of the Lorentzian arc) — is now assembled under the operator-norm Lipschitz seminorm $L_{\mathrm{op}}(a) = \|[\DL, a]\|_{\mathrm{op}}$ on the natural chirality-doubled scalar-multiplier substrate of Paper 44. **Main theorem:** $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(\Tcal^L_{\nmax, \Nt, T}, \Tcal^L_{\Manifold}) \le C_3^{\mathrm{op}}(\nmax) \cdot \gammajoint_{\nmax, \Nt, T} \to 0$ with closed-form $C_3^{\mathrm{op}}(\nmax) = \sqrt{1 - 1/\nmax} = \sqrt{(\nmax - 1)/\nmax} \to 1^-$ and rate $\gammajoint = O(\log \nmax/\nmax + T/\Nt)$ surviving verbatim from Paper 45. **Headline numerical result:** $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(2,3) = 2.0746$, $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(3,5) = 1.6101$, $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(4,7) = 1.3223$ — **bit-exact match with Paper 45's K⁺-weak-form values** (residual $\sim 2.4 \times 10^{-5}$ is the 4-significant-digit rounding in Paper 45 §6 Table 1; underlying $\gamma$ values match to mpmath precision). The "free-upgrade" reading is supported: the strong-form holds on the full Krein space (capturing chirality-flipping commutator content the K⁺-weak-form discards) with the same numerical bound. **Riemannian-limit recovery at $\Nt = 1$ bit-exact** ($0.0$ residual in float64) at $\nmax \in \{2, 3, 4\}$. **Sub-sprint trajectory:** **(L3b-2a — Candidate validation, NO-GO with substantive structural finding.)** The recommended scoping-memo candidate $L_{\mathrm{block}}(a) = \max(\|[\DL, a]|_{\Kplus}\|_{\mathrm{op}}, \|[\DL, a]|_{\Kminus}\|_{\mathrm{op}})$ is identically zero on the natural substrate (all 42 generators at $(2,3)$ and 275 generators at $(3,5)$ give $L_{\mathrm{block}}(a) = 0$ bit-exact). Diagnostic-before-engineering rule converted a 4–6-week planned sprint into a one-day clean negative. **Substantive new content:** $\DL = D_L^{\mathrm{diag}} + D_L^{\mathrm{off}}$ where $D_L^{\mathrm{diag}} = i\gamma^0 \otimes \partial_t$ commutes with every natural-substrate generator ($[\gamma^0, M^{\mathrm{spat}}] = 0$ by Paper 44 Prop 5.1 AND $[\partial_t, M^{\mathrm{temp}}] = 0$ both momentum-diagonal — both factors commute, not just the cross-term as Paper 45 §4.2 Lemma 4.3 used), and $D_L^{\mathrm{off}} = iD_{\mathrm{GV}} \otimes I_{\Nt}$ produces a purely chirality-flipping commutator. **The temporal direction is Lipschitz-invisible on the natural substrate** — sharpens Paper 45 §4.2 Lemma 4.3 from "vanishing time-chirality cross-term" to "vanishing temporal commutator identically". Fallback: Candidate 1 = $L_{\mathrm{op}}$ recommended. - **Sprint L3b-2f-α — Enlarged-substrate scoping for strong-form Lorentzian propinquity (2026-05-22):** **POSITIVE-GO** with substantive structural findings. Tests whether enlarging the operator system to chirality-flipping generators $M$ with $\{J, M\} = 0$ produces genuinely-new strong-form content beyond Paper 46's natural-substrate "free-upgrade" result. **Three independent structural identifications support the verdict:** (1) **L3b-2a structural identity BREAKS** on enlarged substrate at temporal-polynomial degree $p \ge 1$: $[D_L^{\mathrm{diag}}, a^{\mathrm{flip}}]$ becomes proportional to $2W \cdot \omega_k^p$ (non-zero), unlocking the temporal direction in the Lipschitz seminorm. (2) **Strict-strong-form separation established:** Paper 45 K⁺-weak-form $L^+_{\mathrm{P45}}(a^{\mathrm{flip}}) = 0$ identically on chirality-flipping generators (because $P_+ M^{\mathrm{flip}} P_+ = 0$, closed-form), while $L_{\mathrm{op}}(a^{\mathrm{flip}}) > 0$. This is the genuinely-new content beyond Paper 46's natural-substrate reading. (3) **Estimated $\Lambda^{\mathrm{enlarged}}(2, 3) \approx 2.66$** vs Paper 45's $2.0746$, ratio $\sim 1.28$ — analytical estimate consistent with Paper 46 §7.2's predicted $\sqrt{2}$–$2$ constant range. **Construction correction (subtle but load-bearing):** the minimal anti-commuting enlargement in Paper 44's chiral-basis convention is the **chirality-asymmetric doubling $M^{\mathrm{flip}} = \mathrm{diag}(W, -W)$**, NOT the off-block-diagonal form $[[0, W], [W^*, 0]]$ that Paper 46 §7.2 abstractly described — the distinction matters because in Paper 44's chiral basis ($\gamma^0 = [[0, I], [I, 0]]$) the off-block-diagonal form COMMUTES with $\gamma^0$ when $W$ is Hermitian (so does not anti-commute with $J$), while the asymmetric-doubling form ANTI-COMMUTES correctly. - **Sprint Paper 39 k-fold extension — CLOSED (2026-05-23):** Higher tensor factors named open question (Paper 39 §6 (iii)) promoted from "$O(\sqrt k)$ growing constant" to formal theorem at **$k$-INDEPENDENT constant**. **Substantive improvement on the CLAUDE.md estimate.** k-fold tensor-product propinquity convergence on $\mathcal{T}_{S^3}^{\lambda_1} \otimes \cdots \otimes \mathcal{T}_{S^3}^{\lambda_k}$: $\Lambda^{(k)} \le C_3^{(k)} \cdot \gamma^{(k)}$ with **$C_3^{(k)} \le \sqrt{(N_*-1)/(N_*+1)}$ where $N_* = \max_j n_j$ — IDENTICAL to Paper 38 L3 single-factor constant, $k$-independent**, and $\gamma^{(k)} = \max_j \gamma^{\SU(2)}_{n_j}$ (worst-factor SU(2) rate, also $k$-independent). **Mechanism (substantive new content):** k-fold Pythagorean Leibniz identity $\|\sum_j X_j\|^2 = \sum_j \|X_j\|^2$ (sum-of-squares) on the Connes-Marcolli graded module, where the $k$ summands of $D^{(k)} = \sum_j \gamma_{<j} \otimes \DCH^{(j)} \otimes I_{>j}$ pairwise anti-commute. This eliminates the $\sqrt k$ Cauchy-Schwarz factor that a triangle-inequality bound would produce. Per-irrep ratio $\sum_j (N_j-1)^2 / \sum_j (N_j-1)(N_j+1) \le \max_j (N_j-1)/(N_j+1)$ via the rearrangement $\sum a_j^2 = \sum (a_j/b_j) a_j b_j \le \max_j(a_j/b_j) \sum a_j b_j$. Taking square roots gives the closed form. **Net structural finding:** k-fold tensor-product extension introduces ZERO degradation in the Lipschitz comparison constant compared to single-factor — clean drop-in tool for arbitrary multi-focal-composition arguments at any $k$. **Asymptotic $\to 1^-$ as $\min_j n_j \to \infty$** identical to Paper 38 L3 universal $4/\pi$ rate constant. **Five-lemma transport (L1'-T-k through L5-T-k) is mechanical** from Paper 39's two-factor case. **Paper 39 §6 (iii) edit applied** (status updated from "$O(\sqrt k)$ growing" to "CLOSED with k-INDEPENDENT stronger constant"). **Paper 39 compile bug-fix bonus:** during this sprint, six pre-existing double-subscript errors on `\opnorm{T_X}_{\mathrm{cb}}` patterns (introduced at unknown earlier point, made Paper 39 uncompilable) were repaired via new `\cbnorm` macro + `microtype` disable (same fix as Papers 38/40/42/45/46/47 MiKTeX environmental issue). Paper 39 now compiles three-pass clean at 15 pages. **Honest scope:** proof rests on Connes-Marcolli graded Dirac convention (Paper 39 §3.2 — NOT GeoVac's truthful chirality-diagonal $\DCH$); operator-algebraic / qualitative-rate level matching Paper 39's main theorem maturity; off-diagonal cutoff sharpness not addressed (mechanical sup over Avery basis gives the worst-case constant); $k=3$ numerical panel not run (mechanical extension of `geovac/gh_convergence_tensor.py` is sprint-scale follow-on if PI wants empirical confirmation). - **Sprint Pythagorean Orthogonality — formal proof of $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L\rangle_{HS} = 0$ (2026-05-23):** **CLOSED at the operator-algebraic level via $\mathbb{Z}_2$ wedge-chirality parity argument.** Promotes the L2-F.1 (2026-05-17) "structural sketch" of the subspace-decomposition mechanism to a formal Theorem (Paper 43 §10.2 Theorem `thm:pythagorean_formal`), closing the Paper 43 §11 O4 named follow-on. **Theorem:** under the BW construction at finite $(n_{\max}, N_t)$, $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L\rangle_{HS} = \mathrm{Tr}_{\mathcal{K}_W}(H_{\mathrm{local}}^\dagger D_W^L) = 0$ as an exact operator-algebraic identity. **Three structural inputs from Papers 42/43/44:** (I1) wedge chirality grading $\Pi_W$ (BBB $\gamma^5$ restricted to wedge) is a unitary self-adjoint involution; (I2) $[\Pi_W, H_{\mathrm{local}}] = 0$ (even parity — $K_\alpha^W = J_{\mathrm{polar}}^W$ acts by $m_j$-dependent eigenvalues independent of chirality); (I3) $\{\Pi_W, D_W^L\} = 0$ (odd parity — both factors of $D_L = i(\gamma^0 \otimes \partial_t + D_{\mathrm{GV}} \otimes I)$ are $\Pi_W$-odd: $\gamma^0$ anticommutes with $\gamma^5$ in chiral basis; truthful chirality-diagonal $D_{\mathrm{GV}}$ becomes off-diagonal in unfolded-wedge basis via L2-F.1 basis change). **Lemma (parity / HS-orthogonality):** if $\Pi$ is a unitary involution, $[\Pi, A] = 0$, $\{\Pi, B\} = 0$, then $\mathrm{Tr}(A^\dagger B) = 0$ via cyclicity-of-trace and unitary-conjugation invariance ($\mathrm{Tr}(X) = \mathrm{Tr}(\Pi X \Pi^{-1})$). **Net structural finding:** the bit-exact $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L\rangle_{HS} = 0$ at 18 panel cells (L2-F.1) is no longer empirical — it is the exact algebraic identity forced by the BW-construction $\mathbb{Z}_2$ parity grading. Pythagorean closed form $r^2 = \|H_{\mathrm{local}}\|_F^2 + \|D_W^L\|_F^2$ follows as immediate corollary. **Universality across six modular witnesses** (BW + HH×2 + Sew + Unruh×2) is automatic: witnesses parameterize $\kappa_g$ which rescales $H_{\mathrm{local}}$ within its $\Pi_W$-even subspace, cannot rotate it into the $\Pi_W$-odd subspace where $D_W^L$ sits. **Honest scope (preserved):** (i) proof rests on the three structural inputs from Papers 42/43/44 — granular derivation from CH matrix elements is a sub-sprint follow-on; (ii) finite cutoff only, continuum limit requires Paper 47's two-rate hybrid; (iii) wedge only, cross-manifold $T_{S^3} \otimes T_{\mathrm{Hardy}(S^5)}$ remains G3 blocker. **Paper 43 edits applied (same session):** §10.2 promoted from "structural sketch" with named follow-on to formal Theorem block (Lemma `lem:parity_HS` + Theorem `thm:pythagorean_formal` + proof + three inputs I1/I2/I3 + honest scope); §11 O4 status updated from "formal proof named follow-on" to "now formally closed by Theorem `thm:pythagorean_formal`"; Paper 43 grew 24→25 pages, three-pass clean compile, zero substantive warnings. **WH1 PROVEN status maintained** — Pythagorean orthogonality formal proof is structurally additive within the Lorentzian arc (Papers 43 / 45 / 46 / 47), not a re-test of any foundation.
